Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 98, a development version of the Apollo 11 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Luminary 99 revision 1 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The code was then updated by undoing changes described in original Luminary memo 85, using asterisks indicating changed lines in the listing as a guide. While no listing of this version is known to exist, nor are the memory-bank checksums available, the reconstruction is believed to be correct because it was an an intermediate step in reconstructing Luminary 97 whose reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152G. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Luminary 099 revision 001 printout, although the added code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Luminary 98 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

020644,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
020645,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
020646,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 98.
020647,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the a
020648,000006:                                                                                                  ##              development version of the flight software for the Lunar 
020649,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 11.
020650,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Luminary 99
020651,000009:                                                                                                  ##              revision 001, using asterisks indicating changed lines in
020652,000010:                                                                                                  ##              the listing and Luminary Memo #85, which lists changes between
020653,000011:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 98 and 99.
020654,000012:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 492-613
020655,000013:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL

020661,000019:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
020662,000020: 
020663,000021:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020664,000022: 
020665,000023:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
020666,000024:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
020667,000025: 
020668,000026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020669,000027: 
020670,000028:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
020671,000029:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
020672,000030:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
020673,000031:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
020674,000032: 
020675,000033:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020676,000034: 
020677,000035:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
020678,000036: 
020679,000037:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020680,000038: 
020681,000039:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
020682,000040:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
020683,000041:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
020684,000042:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
020685,000043:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
020686,000044:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
020687,000045:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
020688,000046:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
020689,000047:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
020690,000048:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
020691,000049: 
020692,000050:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
020693,000051: 
020694,000052:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020695,000053:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020696,000054: 
020697,000055:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
020698,000056: 
020699,000057:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
020700,000058: 
020701,000059:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020702,000060: 
020703,000061:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
020704,000062: 
020705,000063:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020706,000064: 
020707,000065:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020708,000066: 
020709,000067:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
020710,000068: 
020711,000069:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020712,000070: 
020713,000071:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
020714,000072: 
020715,000073: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
020716,000074: 
020717,000075: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
020718,000076: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
020719,000077: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
020720,000078: 
020721,000079: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020722,000080: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

021130,000488:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021131,000489: 
021132,000490:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021133,000491:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021134,000492:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021135,000493: 
021136,000494:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021137,000495: 
021138,000496:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021139,000497:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021140,000498:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021141,000499:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021142,000500: 
021143,000501:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021144,000502: 
021145,000503:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021146,000504:

021157,000515:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021219,000577:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021220,000578:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021221,000579: 
021222,000580:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021223,000581:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021224,000582: 
021225,000583:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021226,000584: 
021227,000585:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021228,000586:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021229,000587: 
021230,000588:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021231,000589: 
021232,000590:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021233,000591:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021234,000592: 
021235,000593:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021236,000594: 
021237,000595:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021238,000596:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021239,000597:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021240,000598: 
021241,000599:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021242,000600: 
021243,000601:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021244,000602:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021245,000603:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021246,000604: 
021247,000605:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021248,000606: 
021249,000607:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM
021250,000608:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021251,000609: 
021252,000610:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021253,000611: 
021254,000612:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021255,000613: 
021256,000614:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021257,000615: 
021258,000616:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021259,000617: 
021260,000618:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021261,000619: 
021262,000620:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
021263,000621: 
021264,000622:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021265,000623: 
021266,000624:                                                                                                  #        SEE LSR22.1, LSR22.2, LSR22.3
021267,000625: 
021268,000626: 24,2451  E7,1737                                  EBANK=   LRS22.1X

021434,000792:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021435,000793:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021436,000794: 
021437,000795:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021438,000796:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021439,000797: 
021440,000798:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021441,000799: 
021442,000800:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021443,000801:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021444,000802: 
021445,000803:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021446,000804: 
021447,000805:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021448,000806:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021449,000807: 
021450,000808:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021451,000809: 
021452,000810:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021453,000811:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021454,000812:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021455,000813:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021456,000814: 
021457,000815:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021458,000816:                                                                                                  #        
021459,000817:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021460,000818:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021461,000819: 
021462,000820:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021463,000821: 
021464,000822:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021465,000823:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021466,000824:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021467,000825: 
021468,000826:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021469,000827: 
021470,000828:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021471,000829: 
021472,000830:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021473,000831: 
021474,000832:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021475,000833: 
021476,000834:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021477,000835: 
021478,000836:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021479,000837: 
021480,000838:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021481,000839: 
021482,000840:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021483,000841: 
021484,000842: 24,2674  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021485,000843: 24,2674                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021486,000844: 24,2674           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021487,000845: 24,2675           00006                           EXTEND

021664,001022: 
021665,001023:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021666,001024: 
021667,001025:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
021668,001026:

021743,001101:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
021744,001102:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021745,001103: 
021746,001104:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021747,001105:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021748,001106: 
021749,001107:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021750,001108: 
021751,001109:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
021752,001110:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
021753,001111:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
021754,001112: 
021755,001113:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
021756,001114: 
021757,001115:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
021758,001116:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
021759,001117:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
021760,001118:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
021761,001119: 
021762,001120:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021763,001121: 
021764,001122:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
021765,001123:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
021766,001124:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
021767,001125: 
021768,001126:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021769,001127: 
021770,001128:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
021771,001129:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
021772,001130:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
021773,001131: 
021774,001132:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021775,001133: 
021776,001134:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
021777,001135: 
021778,001136:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
021779,001137: 
021780,001138:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
021781,001139: 
021782,001140:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021783,001141: 
021784,001142:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
021785,001143: 
021786,001144:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021787,001145: 
021788,001146:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
021789,001147: 
021790,001148: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
021791,001149: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
021792,001150: 24,3206           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
021793,001151: 24,3207           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
021794,001152: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
021795,001153: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
021796,001154: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
021797,001155: 24,3213           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
021798,001156: 24,3214           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
021799,001157: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

021859,001217:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
021860,001218:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021861,001219: 
021862,001220:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO: 3               DATE: 4-11-67
021863,001221:                                                                                                  #        MOD BY: P VOLANTE   SDC
021864,001222: 
021865,001223:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION -
021866,001224: 
021867,001225:                                                                                                  #        TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
021868,001226:                                                                                                  #        TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
021869,001227:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE.
021870,001228: 
021871,001229:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021872,001230: 
021873,001231:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021874,001232:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R61LEM
021875,001233: 
021876,001234:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021877,001235: 
021878,001236:                                                                                                  #        LPS20.1         VECPOINT
021879,001237:                                                                                                  #        KALCMAN3
021880,001238: 
021881,001239:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021882,001240: 
021883,001241:                                                                                                  #        NORMAL RETURN IS TO CALLER + 1
021884,001242: 
021885,001243:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021886,001244: 
021887,001245:                                                                                                  #        TERMINATE P20 + R61 BY BRANCHING TO P20END IF BOTH TRACKFLAG +
021888,001246:                                                                                                  #        RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.
021889,001247: 
021890,001248:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -

022068,001426:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022069,001427: 
022070,001428:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022071,001429: 
022072,001430:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022073,001431:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022074,001432:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022075,001433:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022076,001434:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022077,001435: 
022078,001436:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022079,001437:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022080,001438:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022081,001439:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022082,001440: 
022083,001441:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022084,001442:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022085,001443:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022086,001444:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022087,001445:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022088,001446: 
022089,001447:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022090,001448: 
022091,001449:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022092,001450:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022093,001451: 
022094,001452:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022095,001453: 
022096,001454:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022097,001455:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022098,001456:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022099,001457: 
022100,001458:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022101,001459: 
022102,001460:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022103,001461: 
022104,001462:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022105,001463: 
022106,001464:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022107,001465:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022108,001466: 
022109,001467:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022152,001510:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022153,001511: 
022154,001512:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022155,001513:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022156,001514:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022157,001515:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022158,001516:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022159,001517:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022160,001518:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022161,001519:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022162,001520:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022163,001521:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022164,001522:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022165,001523:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022166,001524:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022167,001525:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022168,001526:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022169,001527:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022170,001528:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022171,001529:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022172,001530:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022173,001531:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022174,001532: 
022175,001533:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022176,001534:

022178,001536: 
022179,001537:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022180,001538: 
022181,001539:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022182,001540: 
022183,001541:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022184,001542: 
022185,001543:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022224,001582:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022225,001583: 
022226,001584:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022227,001585: 
022228,001586:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022229,001587:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022230,001588:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022231,001589:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022232,001590:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022233,001591:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022234,001592:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022235,001593:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022236,001594:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022237,001595:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022238,001596:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022239,001597:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022240,001598: 
022241,001599:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022242,001600:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022243,001601:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022244,001602: 
022245,001603:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022246,001604: 
022247,001605:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022248,001606: 
022249,001607:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022250,001608:

022252,001610:                                                                                                  #

022254,001612: 
022255,001613:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)

022273,001631:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022274,001632: 
022275,001633:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022276,001634:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022277,001635:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022278,001636:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022279,001637:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022280,001638:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022281,001639:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022282,001640:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022283,001641:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022284,001642:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022285,001643:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022286,001644:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022287,001645:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022288,001646:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022289,001647:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022290,001648:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022291,001649: 
022292,001650:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022293,001651: 
022294,001652:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022295,001653: 
022296,001654:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022297,001655: 
022298,001656:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022299,001657: 
022300,001658:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022301,001659: 
022302,001660:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022303,001661: 
022304,001662:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022305,001663: 
022306,001664:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022307,001665:

022311,001669: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022312,001670: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU

022349,001707:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022350,001708: 
022351,001709:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022352,001710: 
022353,001711:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022354,001712:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022355,001713:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022356,001714:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022357,001715:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022358,001716:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022359,001717:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022360,001718:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022361,001719:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022362,001720:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022363,001721:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022364,001722:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022365,001723:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022366,001724:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022367,001725:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022368,001726:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022369,001727:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022370,001728:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022371,001729:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022372,001730:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022373,001731:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022374,001732:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022375,001733: 
022376,001734:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022377,001735: 
022378,001736:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022379,001737:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022380,001738: 
022381,001739:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022382,001740: 
022383,001741:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022384,001742: 
022385,001743:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022386,001744: 
022387,001745:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022388,001746: 
022389,001747:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022390,001748: 
022391,001749:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022392,001750: 
022393,001751:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022394,001752: 
022395,001753:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES

022442,001800:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022443,001801: 
022444,001802:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022445,001803:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022446,001804:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022447,001805:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022448,001806:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022449,001807:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022450,001808:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022451,001809:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022452,001810:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022453,001811:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022454,001812:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022455,001813:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022456,001814:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022457,001815:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022458,001816:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022459,001817:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022460,001818:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022461,001819:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022462,001820:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022463,001821:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022464,001822: 
022465,001823:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022466,001824: 
022467,001825:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022468,001826:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022469,001827:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022470,001828:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022471,001829: 
022472,001830:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022473,001831: 
022474,001832:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022475,001833:

022481,001839:

022539,001897:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022540,001898: 
022541,001899:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022542,001900: 
022543,001901:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022544,001902:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022545,001903:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022546,001904:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022547,001905:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022548,001906:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022549,001907:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022550,001908:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022551,001909:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022552,001910:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022553,001911:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022554,001912:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022555,001913:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022556,001914:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022557,001915: 
022558,001916:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022559,001917:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022560,001918:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022561,001919:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022562,001920:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022563,001921:

022632,001990:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
022633,001991: 
022634,001992:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022635,001993: 
022636,001994:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
022637,001995:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
022638,001996:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
022639,001997:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
022640,001998:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
022641,001999:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
022642,002000:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
022643,002001:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
022644,002002:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
022645,002003:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
022646,002004:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
022647,002005:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
022648,002006:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022649,002007: 
022650,002008:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022651,002009:                                                                                                  #        
022652,002010:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
022653,002011:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

022742,002100:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
022743,002101: 
022744,002102:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022745,002103: 
022746,002104:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
022747,002105:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
022748,002106:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
022749,002107:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
022750,002108:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
022751,002109:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
022752,002110:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
022753,002111:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
022754,002112:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
022755,002113:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
022756,002114:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
022757,002115:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
022758,002116:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
022759,002117:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
022760,002118:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
022761,002119:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
022762,002120:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
022763,002121:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
022764,002122:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022765,002123:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
022766,002124:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
022767,002125:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
022768,002126: 
022769,002127:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022770,002128: 
022771,002129:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
022772,002130:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
022773,002131:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022774,002132:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022775,002133: 
022776,002134:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022777,002135: 
022778,002136:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
022779,002137:

022781,002139:

022783,002141:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV

022832,002190:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
022833,002191: 
022834,002192:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
022835,002193:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
022836,002194:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022837,002195:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
022838,002196:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
022839,002197:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022840,002198:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
022841,002199:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
022842,002200:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
022843,002201:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
022844,002202:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
022845,002203:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
022846,002204:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
022847,002205:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
022848,002206:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
022849,002207:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
022850,002208:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
022851,002209:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
022852,002210:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
022853,002211:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
022854,002212:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022855,002213: 
022856,002214:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022857,002215: 
022858,002216:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
022859,002217: 
022860,002218:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
