023005,002363:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023006,002364: 
023007,002365:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023008,002366: 
023009,002367:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023010,002368:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023011,002369:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023012,002370:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023013,002371:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023014,002372:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023015,002373:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023016,002374:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023017,002375:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023018,002376:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023019,002377:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023020,002378:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023021,002379:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023022,002380:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023023,002381:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023024,002382:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023025,002383:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023026,002384:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023027,002385:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023028,002386:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023029,002387:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023030,002388:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023031,002389:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023032,002390:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023033,002391:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023034,002392: 
023035,002393:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023036,002394: 
023037,002395:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023038,002396:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023039,002397:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023040,002398: 
023041,002399:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023042,002400:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023043,002401: 
023044,002402:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023045,002403:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023046,002404: 
023047,002405:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023048,002406: 
023049,002407:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023050,002408:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023051,002409: 
023052,002410:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023053,002411:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023054,002412:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023055,002413: 
023056,002414: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023100,002458:

Page 547 

023102,002460:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023103,002461: 
023104,002462:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023105,002463: 
023106,002464:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023107,002465:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023108,002466:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023109,002467:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023110,002468:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023111,002469:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023112,002470:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023113,002471:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023114,002472:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023115,002473:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023116,002474:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023117,002475:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023118,002476:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023119,002477:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023120,002478:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023121,002479:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023122,002480:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023123,002481:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023124,002482:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023125,002483:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023126,002484:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023127,002485:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023128,002486:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023129,002487:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023130,002488:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023131,002489:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023132,002490:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023133,002491:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023134,002492:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023135,002493:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023136,002494:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023137,002495:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023138,002496:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023139,002497:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023140,002498:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023141,002499:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023142,002500:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023143,002501: 
023144,002502:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023145,002503: 
023146,002504:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023147,002505: 
023148,002506:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023149,002507: 
023150,002508:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023151,002509:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023152,002510: 
023153,002511:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023154,002512: 
023155,002513:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 548 

023157,002515: 
023158,002516:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023159,002517: 
023160,002518:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023161,002519: 
023162,002520:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023163,002521: 
023164,002522:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023165,002523: 
023166,002524: 25,2636           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023167,002525: 25,2637           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023168,002526: 25,2640           53110                           DXCH     TANG                                  
023169,002527: 
023170,002528: 25,2641           06037                           TC       INTPRET                               
023171,002529: 
023172,002530: 25,2642           77201                           SETPD    VLOAD

023771,003129:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
023772,003130:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
023773,003131: 
023774,003132:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023775,003133:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
023776,003134:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
023777,003135:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
023778,003136: 
023779,003137:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
023780,003138:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
023781,003139: 
023782,003140:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023783,003141:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
023784,003142: 
023785,003143:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
023786,003144: 
023787,003145:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
023788,003146: 
023789,003147:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023790,003148: 
023791,003149:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
023792,003150:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
023793,003151:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
023794,003152:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
023795,003153: 
023796,003154:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
023797,003155:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
023798,003156:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
023799,003157: 
023800,003158:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
023801,003159:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
023802,003160: 
023803,003161: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
023804,003162: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
023805,003163: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

023807,003165: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
023808,003166: 
023809,003167: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
023810,003168: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
023811,003169: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
023812,003170: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
023813,003171: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE
023814,003172: 24,3262           04307                                    SURFFLAG                              #  DON'T CALL LEMCONIC
023815,003173: 24,3263           51274                                    CSMINT                                
023816,003174: 24,3264           77624        LMINT              CALL                                           
023817,003175: 24,3265           27100                                    LEMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE LEM
023818,003176: 24,3266           77775                           VLOAD                                          
023819,003177: 24,3267           00001                                    RATT                                  
023820,003178: 24,3270           26352                           STOVL    LMPOS                                 #  SAVE LM POSITION B-29
023821,003179: 24,3271           00007                                    VATT                                  
023822,003180: 24,3272           16360                           STODL    LMVEL                                 #  SAVE LM VELOCITY B-7
023823,003181: 24,3273           00015                                    TAT                                   
023824,003182: 24,3274           34041        CSMINT             STCALL   TDEC1                                 
023825,003183: 24,3275           27066                                    CSMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE CSM
023826,003184: 24,3276           52375                           VLOAD    VSU                                   #  COMPUTE RELATIVE VELOCITY V(CSM) - V(LM)
023827,003185: 24,3277           00007                                    VATT                                  
023828,003186: 24,3300           02360                                    LMVEL                                 
023829,003187: 24,3301           76521                           MXV      VSL1                                  
023830,003188: 24,3302           01734                                    REFSMMAT

023900,003258:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
023901,003259:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
023902,003260: 
023903,003261:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023904,003262:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
023905,003263:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
023906,003264:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
023907,003265:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
023908,003266: 
023909,003267:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
023910,003268: 
023911,003269:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023912,003270:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
023913,003271:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
023914,003272:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
023915,003273:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
023916,003274: 
023917,003275:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
023918,003276: 
023919,003277:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
023920,003278:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
023921,003279:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
023922,003280: 
023923,003281:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
023924,003282:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
023925,003283: 
023926,003284:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
023927,003285:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
023928,003286: 
023929,003287:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
023930,003288:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
023931,003289:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
023932,003290:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
023933,003291:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS

024124,003482:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024125,003483:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024126,003484:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024127,003485: 
024128,003486:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024129,003487:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024130,003488:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024131,003489:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024132,003490: 
024133,003491:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024134,003492:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024135,003493:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024136,003494:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024137,003495:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024138,003496:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024139,003497:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024140,003498: 
024141,003499:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024142,003500:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024143,003501:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024144,003502: 
024145,003503:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024146,003504:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024147,003505:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024148,003506:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024149,003507:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024150,003508:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024151,003509: 
024152,003510:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024153,003511:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024154,003512:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024155,003513:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024156,003514:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024157,003515:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024158,003516:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024159,003517:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024160,003518:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024161,003519:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024162,003520:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024163,003521:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024164,003522:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024165,003523:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024166,003524:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024167,003525: 
024168,003526:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024169,003527:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024170,003528:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

024172,003530:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

024565,003923: 
024566,003924:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024567,003925:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
024568,003926:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
024569,003927:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024570,003928: 
024571,003929:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024572,003930:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
024573,003931:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
024574,003932: 
024575,003933:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024576,003934:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024577,003935:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

024579,003937:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
024580,003938:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024581,003939:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024582,003940: 
024583,003941:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024584,003942:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024585,003943:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024586,003944:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024587,003945:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024588,003946:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
024589,003947:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG

024695,004053: 
024696,004054:                                                                                                  #  GETULC
024697,004055: 
024698,004056:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM
024699,004057:                                                                                                  #  AND THE LM, LEAVING THE UNIT VECTOR IN THE PUSHLIST AND MPAC AND THE

024724,004082: 
024725,004083:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
024726,004084: 
024727,004085:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

024789,004147:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
024790,004148:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
024791,004149: 
024792,004150:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024793,004151: 
024794,004152:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
024795,004153:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
024796,004154:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
024797,004155:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
024798,004156: 
024799,004157:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
024800,004158:

024806,004164:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
024807,004165:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL

025042,004400:

Page 594 

025044,004402:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025045,004403:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025046,004404: 
025047,004405:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025048,004406: 
025049,004407:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025050,004408:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025051,004409:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025052,004410:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025053,004411:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025054,004412:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025055,004413: 
025056,004414:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025057,004415: 
025058,004416:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025059,004417: 
025060,004418:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025061,004419:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025062,004420:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025063,004421:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025064,004422:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025065,004423:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025066,004424: 
025067,004425:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025068,004426: 
025069,004427:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025070,004428: 
025071,004429:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025072,004430:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025073,004431:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025074,004432:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025075,004433:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 595 

025077,004435: 
025078,004436:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025079,004437: 
025080,004438:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025081,004439:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025082,004440:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025083,004441:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025084,004442: 
025085,004443:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025086,004444: 
025087,004445:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)

025274,004632:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025275,004633: 
025276,004634:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025277,004635:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025278,004636:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025279,004637:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025280,004638:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025281,004639: 
025282,004640:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025283,004641:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025284,004642: 
025285,004643: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025286,004644: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025287,004645: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025288,004646: 
025289,004647: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025290,004648: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025291,004649: 
025292,004650: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025293,004651: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025294,004652: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025295,004653: 
025296,004654: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025297,004655: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025298,004656: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025299,004657: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025300,004658: 
025301,004659: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025302,004660: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025303,004661: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025304,004662: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025305,004663: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025306,004664: 
025307,004665: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025308,004666: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025309,004667: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025310,004668: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025311,004669: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025312,004670: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025313,004671: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025314,004672: 
025315,004673: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025316,004674: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025317,004675: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025318,004676: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025319,004677: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025320,004678: 
025321,004679: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025322,004680: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025323,004681:

Page 601 

025325,004683:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025326,004684:

025361,004719:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
